This is the v1.15 version of CP/M 3 for PCW 8256 and later old world
machines.

0003: 31 00 cf		LD SP, &CF00		; SP <- &CF00
0006: 21 f0 ff		LD HL, &FFF0		; blank memory from
0009: 11 f1 ff		LD DE, &FFF1		; &fff0 -> &ffff
000c: 01 0f 00		LD BC, &000F
000e: 36 00		LD (HL), &00
0011: ed b0		LDIR

0013: 3e 84		LD A, &84		; Page 4
0015: d3 f3		OUT (&F3), A		; .. in &C000->FFFF

; Looks like this is blanking RAM in each page
0017: 21 00 c0		LD HL, &C000
001a: 11 01 c0		LD DE, &C001
001d: 01 ff 3f		LD BC, &3FFF
0020: 75		LD (HL), L		; c000 <- 0
0021: FE 89		CP &89
0023: 20 02		JR NZ, ...
0025: 36		INC H
0026: e5		PUSH HL
0027: ed b0		LDIR
0029: 3c		INC A
002a: fe 90		CP &90
002c: 20 e7		JR NZ, ...

002e: 3e 88		LD A, &88		; Page 8 (CCP, buffers, more BIOS)
0030: d3 f3		OUT (&F3), A		; .. in &C000->FFFF

0032: 21 fe 60		LD HL, &60FE

0038: 01 80 0c		LD BC, &0C80

004c: 3e 87		LD A, &87		; Page 7 (common?)
004e: d3 f3		OUT (&F3), A		; .. in &C000->&FFFF

0050: 21 d7 29		LD HL, &29D7

0056: 01 27 07		LD BC, &0727
0059: ed b0		LDIR

005b: 11 00 cd		LD DE, &CD00		; Copy &006B -> &CD00
005e: d5		PUSH DE			; Save to RET into
005f: 21 6b 00		LD HL, &006B
0062: 01 26 01		LD BC, &0126		; &126 bytes
0065: ed b0		LDIR

0067: 3a 00 00		LD A, (&0000)	; .. this is &01 ? Why?
006a: c9		RET		; pop de, continue execution at &CD00
